     <script>
      var shouldLoadBasket = window.location.search.indexOf("loadBasket");
    if (shouldLoadBasket !== -1) {
      loadBasket();
    }

    function setupBasket() {  
      if (window.loadMinibasketAssets) {
        loadBasket();
      // } else {
      //   window.addEventListener('jl-events.browser.showMinibasket', loadBasket);
      }
    }

    function loadBasket() {
      if (window.isMinibasketBundleLoaded !== true) {
        const scriptVendor = document.createElement('script');
        scriptVendor.src = '/show-basket-ui/minibasket/dist/MinibasketApp.Vendors.js';
        scriptVendor.defer = true;
        document.head.appendChild(scriptVendor);
        
        const script = document.createElement('script');
        script.src = '/show-basket-ui/minibasket/dist/MinibasketApp.js';
        script.defer = true;
        document.head.appendChild(script);
        
        window.isMinibasketBundleLoaded = true;
      }
    }

    function handleBasketButtonClick(event) {
      if (window.isMinibasketLoaded) {
        event.preventDefault();
        const customEvent = new window.CustomEvent(
          'jl-events.browser.showMinibasket',
          {
            detail: {
              source: 'page-level',
            },
          }
        );
        window.dispatchEvent(customEvent);
      }
  }

       <script>
        (function (){
            var button = document.querySelector('#signup-footer-banner-button .c-button');

            var loadScript = function (src) {
                var script = document.createElement('script');
                script.src = src;
                document.head.appendChild(script);
            };

            // React Modal needs to know the id of the application so it can hide it from screenreaders when the modal is open
            // Ideally this banner will be used on an application that has a root id of 'root', but if it doesn't we'll add one
            // if (!document.getElementById('root')) {
                // document.querySelector('[data-assembly-source="signup/footer-banner"]').id = 'root';
            // }

            var loadScripts = function () {
                loadScript('/signup/public/bundle.js');
                loadScript('/signup/public/footer-banner.js');
            };
            
            button.addEventListener('click', function () {
                button.classList.add('c-button--submitting');
                
                loadScripts();
            });

            if (window.location.search.indexOf('signup=true') > -1) {
                loadScripts();
            }

            var rebuildTheBase = {};
            
            rebuildTheBase.signup = function (source) {
                // this source will be read by the application later
                rebuildTheBase.signup.source = source;

                loadScripts();
            };

            window.rebuildTheBase = rebuildTheBase;
        }());
       </script>
